        // Filter query
        var sQueryFiltered = $("#site-search-1754967 input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#site-search-1754967 input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );

            return true;
        }else{
            return false;

    <script>
     jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                        var sNavContainer = '#site-navbar-container';
                        var sBodyContainer = '.offcanvas-inner';
                        var sNavHeight = $(sNavContainer).height();
                        var iUnfixPoint = 0;
                        
                        if( __tnt.client.platform.ios ){
                            $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix-sticky');
                        } else {
                            $sNavScroll = false;
                            $(window).on('DOMMouseScroll mousewheel', function(e){
                                if( !$sNavScroll ){
                                    $sNavScroll = true;
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        var iFixPoint = $(sNavContainer).offset().top;
                                        var iCurrPoint = $(this).scrollTop();
                                        if( iCurrPoint >= iFixPoint && iCurrPoint > iUnfixPoint ){
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix') ){ 
                                                iUnfixPoint = iFixPoint;
                                                $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix').removeClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', sNavHeight+'px'); 
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix-top') ){ 
                                                $(sNavContainer).removeClass('affix').addClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        
                                        $sNavScroll = false;
                                    }, 25);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
    </script>

                     Times Staff

                    return function(){
                        var context = this, args = arguments;
                        var later = function(){
                            timeout = null;
                            func.apply(context, args);
                        };
                        clearTimeout(timeout);
                        timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
                    }

           <script>
            jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                    var assetTracked = [];
                    var isUserAction = false;

                    function trackActive(owl){
                        if( assetTracked.length == 10 ){
                            return;
                        }else{
                            var activeThings = $(owl).find('.owl-item.active');

                            $.each(activeThings, function(index, value){
                                var assetId = $(this).find('.card').data('id');
                                var hasBeenLogged = false;
                                
                                assetTracked.forEach(function (item, index, array) {
                                    if(item == assetId){
                                        hasBeenLogged = true;
                                        return true;
                                    }
                                });
                                if( hasBeenLogged == false ){
                                    assetTracked.push(assetId);
                                    TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                                        app: 'classifieds',
                                        metric: 'featured',
                                        id: assetId
                                    });
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }

                    window.card_carousel_1754996 = $('#block-1754996 .owl-carousel');

                    card_carousel_1754996.on('initialized.owl.carousel', function(e){
                            trackActive(card_carousel_1754996);
                        });
                    
                    
                    card_carousel_1754996.owlCarousel({
                        autoplay:__tnt.client.touchOnly ? false : true,
                        autoplayTimeout:3000,
                        autoplayHoverPause:true,
                        loop:true,
                        margin:15,
                        nav:false,
                        dots:false,
                        slideBy: 'page',
                        autoHeight:false,
                        responsiveClass:true,
                        responsiveBaseElement: '#featured-classifieds-1754996',
                        responsive:{
                            0:{
                                items:1,
                                stagePadding: 40,
                                nav:false
                            },
                            600:{
                                items:1
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    // bind previous click
                    $('#block-1754996 .owl-carousel-control.prev').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(e){
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        card_carousel_1754996.trigger('prev.owl.carousel');
                        
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_1754996);
                    });

                    // bind next click
                    $('#block-1754996 .owl-carousel-control.next').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(e){
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        card_carousel_1754996.trigger('next.owl.carousel');
                        
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_1754996);
                    });

                    // bind dragged
                    card_carousel_1754996.on('dragged.owl.carousel', function(event){
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_1754996);
                    });

                    // bind translated
                    card_carousel_1754996.on('translated.owl.carousel', function(event){
                        if( isUserAction ){
                            trackActive(card_carousel_1754996);
                            isUserAction = false;
                        }
                    });
                });
           </script>

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

   /*<![CDATA[*/ jQuery(document).ready(function($){
        var sTrackingPattern = 'lee-track-';
        var oTrackBlocks = $('div[class*="'+sTrackingPattern+'"]');
        var sTrackVal;
        function lee_trkLinkSrc(o, src){
            var src = 'tracking-source='+src;
            $(o).find('a').each(function(){
                var sHref = this.href;
                var sOg = $(this).attr('href');
                if (!sHref.match(/[#&]tracking-source/) && sHref != '' && sHref != '#' && sOg.charAt(0) == '/') {
                    sHref += ((sHref.indexOf('#') > -1) ? '&' : '#') + src;
                    $(this).attr('href', sHref);
                }
            });
        }
        if( oTrackBlocks.length > 0 ){
            $(oTrackBlocks).each(function(){
                var sTrackClass = $(this)[0].classList;
                $(sTrackClass).each(function(i,c){
                    if( c.match(sTrackingPattern) ){
                        sTrackVal = c.replace(sTrackingPattern, '');
                        return false;
                    }
                });
                lee_trkLinkSrc(this, sTrackVal);
            });
        }
        lee_trkLinkSrc('#main-nav_menu', 'main-nav');
        lee_trkLinkSrc('#mobile-nav-left_menu,#mobile-nav-left-below_menu', 'menu-nav');
